                <div v-if="item.type !== 'wz'" class="match-details-listing__gameIcon" :style="{backgroundImage: 'url(https://www.callofduty.com/cdn/app/icons/' + item.gameMode + ')' }"></div>

                <div v-else class="match-details-listing__gameIcon" :style="{backgroundImage: 'url(https://www.callofduty.com/cdn/app/icons/mw/modes/wz_br.png)' }"></div>

                    <div class="match-details-listing__map">{{ item.map }}</div>
                    <div class="match-details-listing__mode">{{ item.mode }}</div>
                    <div class="match-details-listing__timestamp">{{ item.timestamp | prettyDate }}</div>
                    <div v-if="item.quit === 'true' || item.result === 'quit'" class="match-details-listing__placement quit">
                        <span>-</span>
                    </div>
                    <div v-else class="match-details-listing__placement" :class="[item.type, {loss: item.result !== 'win' && item.gametype !== 'zm'}]">
                        <span v-if="item.gametype === 'wz' && item.mode !== 'Solo'">{{ (item.teamPlacement) ? item.teamPlacement : "-" }}</span>
                        <span v-else-if="item.gametype === 'wz' && item.mode === 'Solo'">{{ (item.playerPlacement) ? item.playerPlacement : "-" }}</span>
                        <span v-else-if="item.gametype === 'zm'">{{ (item.rounds) ? item.rounds : "-" }}</span>
                        <span v-else>{{ (item.result === "win") ? "W" : "L"}}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </li>
        </ul>

    </div>

                             <script>
                              ATVI.library.withDependency('wtb-component', function() {
	        var wtbBundleBuyButtonStatus = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.bundleBuyButtonStatus = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.bundleBuyButtonStatus || [];
    	    var wtbBundlesId = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesId = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesId || [];
        	var wtbBundlesLabel = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesLabel = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesLabel || [];
	        var bundleNode = {id: "physical"};
    	    bundleNode.buttonOverride = false;

        	if (bundleNode.buttonOverride) {
	            bundleNode.buttonValue = "default";
    	        bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = "all";
        	    bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms;
            	bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms.split(",");
	            bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = $.map(bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms, $.trim);
    	    }

            wtbBundleBuyButtonStatus.push(bundleNode);
            wtbBundlesId.push("physical");
            wtbBundlesLabel.push("Physical Standard");
        });
                             </script>
                             <script>
                              ATVI.library.withDependency('wtb-component', function() {

    	    var wtbBundlesId = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesId = ATVI.components.wheretobuy.wtbBundlesId || [];

    	    bundleNode.buttonOverride = false;

        	if (bundleNode.buttonOverride) {
	            bundleNode.buttonValue = "default";
    	        bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = "all";
        	    bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms;
            	bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms.split(",");
	            bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms = $.map(bundleNode.buttonOverridePlatforms, $.trim);
    	    }

            wtbBundleBuyButtonStatus.push(bundleNode);
            wtbBundlesId.push("digital");
            wtbBundlesLabel.push("Digital Standard");
        });
